NEXT:
  current progress
  The Dockerfile has been created with all necessary dependencies installed (OpenJDK 8, Ant, CMake, GCC/G++, GMP libraries, Git, wget, Python3). JAR files have been downloaded successfully. The build failed due to a syntax error in the heredoc section where the environment_check.sh script is being created - the echo commands are being interpreted as Dockerfile instructions instead of being part of the script content.
  next step
  Fix the heredoc syntax in the Dockerfile by properly escaping or reformatting the environment_check.sh creation section. The RUN command with cat and heredoc needs to be written as a single RUN instruction, ensuring all the echo commands are part of the script content, not separate Dockerfile instructions. This can be done by using a different approach such as using printf or echo with proper escaping, or by creating the file with multiple echo commands in a single RUN instruction.
